Former Haizhou Transportation Official Blackmailed by Subordinates 100

Allegations of Private Gain and Corruption

$400 Ransom Demanded

Evidence Returned

Two Arrested On Site

Zhang Tianji, a native of Nanhai County, Guangdong Province, served as the Haizhou Transportation Official. His brother, Zean (An Qinsheng), also served as a section chief in the Transportation Official's office. Last year, Tianji left his post, and the brothers brought their families to Shanghai, residing on Beinan Road. Zean then joined the Zhihua Hospital on Wenzhou Road.

On March 26th of this year, Zean received a letter to be forwarded to Tianji. After reading it, it stated that Tianji had engaged in private gain and corruption while in office. Written evidence had been obtained and would be reported to a superior official, unless 400 yuan was paid as a "birthday gift", after which the evidence would be returned. The letter was signed Zheng Fuyu. Tianji knew that Zheng was the document section chief of the Transportation Official's office, so he ignored what appeared to be blackmail. Zheng then visited Tianji's residence to discuss the matter, but with no result.

A few days ago, Zhang asked his friend Dong Peizhi to rent room 77 at the Hongkou Hotel on North Sichuan Road and invited Zheng to negotiate there. Meanwhile, Zhang sent Zheng's letter to the Municipal Police Headquarters, accusing Zheng of extortion. A detective chief dispatched detectives Zhu Asan and Bao Tang Yao Changmin to wait at the hotel at 9:00 PM. Later, Zheng and his friend Lu Yuquan arrived at the Hongkou Hotel to negotiate with Dong. Dong gave them 400 yuan in marked bills, and Zheng and Lu returned the written evidence. As they left, the detectives pursued and arrested them. The 400 yuan they had extorted had already been split, with Zheng receiving 300 yuan and Lu receiving 100 yuan. Both amounts were found on their persons.

The next morning, they were taken to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Wu questioned them. The plaintiffs, Zhang Tianji and his brother, and the witness Dong Peizhi, testified to the events. Zheng, a native of Shaoxing, stated that he had previously served as Zhang Tianji's document section chief. More than 1,000 yuan in rewards for anti-smuggling confiscated by the Transportation Official's office were embezzled by Zhang when he left his post. He claimed he was entitled to 300 yuan of these rewards, so he asked for it. As for the various acts of corruption during Zhang's tenure, he had listed the evidence and reported it to the Salt Administration of the Ministry of Finance, not extorting him. Lu, a native of Fujian, claimed that he had been trying to resolve the dispute between Zhang and Zheng and that Dong had given him 100 yuan as a reward, which he had refused. The court ordered the two defendants to be remanded in custody for a further hearing.

Heavily in Debt Due To Gambling

were found on his person.

losing every day. 104

Opinion On "Egg Inside an Egg" 108

Related To The Chicken's Constitution

Not A Different Internal Structure

Two hens raised at the Chen Longxing rice store on Sanguantang Street in Tangqiao, Pudong, have laid a total of three "egg-in-egg" eggs, varying in shape and length. Nearby residents have expressed their surprise. This newspaper reported the matter on the 29th of last month. Yesterday, we met Mr. Chen Peide, a former senior executive at an egg factory, who has considerable experience in egg research. We now record his opinion on "egg-in-egg", for the reference of the physiology community.

Mr. Chen said, this is not surprising. The laying of eggs by chickens varies with the constitution. So, there is often a double yolk egg, or an egg with white but no yolk, or a soft egg, etc. Ordinary people see this as strange, but in fact, double yolk eggs are due to the chicken's strong body and excessive essence. Eggs with white but no yolk, and soft eggs, are due to the chicken's weak constitution and incomplete development. "Egg-in-egg" is also due to the hen's excessive appetite, resulting in too much internal lime and essence, and the eggshell being overly fertilized. However, "egg-in-egg" often occurs within the egg yolk cell, and more often in the spring, but cannot be hatched. The chickens at the shop eat rice all day long, so their constitution is strong and their appetite is huge, which can explain the occurence. The eggshell is hard, which can prove that the hen is producing a lot, and it's not that the chicken has a different internal structure. If the chicken is fed less, then "egg-in-egg" will not occur again. It is also said that this kind of "egg-in-egg" can cure blocked digestion, but it remains to be verified.

Dragon Boats Still Seen In Puzhong 109

Wang Chengbao Disregards Prohibition

Luo Sanlong Scams Under A False Identity

According to the old custom, every year during the Dragon Boat Festival, the residents along the river will have dragon boat races, but these old customs were mostly started by unemployed people who were only drumming up support as an excuse to collect money. There were even incidents of drowning during the flag snatching competitions. The government had issued strict prohibitions many times, but those people disobeyed. Yesterday was the Dragon Boat Festival, those people petitioned the Public Security Bureau last month to hold it, but the Fifth District Party Branch did not agree and it was still banned.

The Public Security Bureau ordered the Water Patrol Team to strictly prohibit it and issued a notice. However, at around 7:00 AM yesterday, numerous dragon boats were found at Puyi Ferry and Yangjia Ferry. Captain Xu of the Water Patrol Team dispatched patrol leader Li Chenghua with several police officers to arrest five. After a thorough investigation, Wang Chengbao, the organizer, claimed that the dragon boat race was being done by the people, but after the Public Security Bureau ordered the race to be stopped, Luo Sanlong approached him on May 24, claiming that he could contact the police for 400 yuan to allow the race. Wang agreed and paid 190 yuan on the spot, another 75 yuan was paid on May 30.

Wang said he had paid 265 yuan to Luo, and the money was given to Luo at the Deyi Teahouse in the City God Temple. They realized they were defrauded by Luo now that they were arrested. Captain Xu said that dragon boats do not fit with the nation and they were banned by the Public Security Bureau, and now he realized that they were guilty. He realized that Luo Sanlong dared to impersonate the authorities in order to scam money, which was even more heinous. Other than ordering his men to arrest Luo Sanlong, he sent Wang Chengbao to the judicial branch for approval.

Disaster When Japanese Ship Sinks Rice Boat 110

One Child Drowned

More than 3000 Yuan In Losses

On the morning of May 31, the Xiechangde rice shop in Shanghai North District hired Jia Qiaonan's lighter to transport 210 bags of Saigon rice from the Tongchunfu warehouse in Pudong. At 11:55 AM, while passing through the Huangpu River off the Bund of Nanjing Road, it was struck by the "Kanda Maru" of the Japanese Yamashita Steamship Company. At the same time, the lighter was hooked by an iron hook on the ship. The ship did not stop, but dragged it for 4-5 li. The ship broke, and all the rice fell into the river. The ten people on board cried out. The steamer ignored them. One of the boatman's sons drowned. One of the coolies swam ashore, and the other eight were rescued by the ship's rope ladder. The Jianghai Customs Water Patrol and the Municipal Public Security Bureau Water Patrol witnessed the incident, but due to the speed of the ship, rescue was impossible. Afterwards, the Water Patrol supervised the salvage and retrieved 21 bags of wet rice. The total loss was more than 3,600 yuan. The Bean and Rice Industry Association North Office has sent a serious letter to the Yamashita Company to negotiate.

Illegal Behavior of Defendant's Lawyer in Extortion Case 111

Statement of the police barrister

Stated two illegal acts

Zhou Dingwen, owner of the Zhou Dingji lacquer shop on Gansu Road, was extorted by a letter from bandits. The police arrested Wang Mingfu and Wang Desheng, and their confessions were reported in the newspapers. Judge Sun of the Special District Local Court continued the hearing on the case the other day. Wang Yaotang, the police barrister, suddenly mentioned the illegal behavior of the defendant's lawyer, Da Yaoxian.

The defense lawyer for a defendant in a criminal case should obtain permission from the police barrister or the police chief or the Western investigator in charge of the case before contacting his client in detention. However, lawyer Da entered the detention center without going through the above procedures. When questioned by the Chinese police, he falsely claimed to have obtained permission. This is one illegal act. After his client signed the statement, Lawyer Da instructed him not to confess anything during the court hearing.

The Chinese police heard this, this is the second illegal act. He specially made a solemn statement and requested the court to investigate it. Lawyer Da also immediately defended himself and denied any illegal behavior. Judge Sun ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody for another hearing in seven days. Regarding the part of concealing criminals, it will be sent to the prosecutor for investigation.

Zhuang Jian'an Responds To Dispute With Yicheng Steamship Company 112

Denies Fraudulent Behavior

Wang Hancai Was In Fact A Partner

Zhuang Jian'an, the brother of Zhuang Dezhi, chairman of the Shanghai Commercial and Savings Bank, organized the Yicheng Steamship Company last year and rented the Hanping steamship. He hired a comprador, which was filled by Zhuang Zhongcai. Wang Hancai was the deputy comprador. The security deposit of 2,000 yuan should have been attached to the comprador's security deposit. Zhuang guaranteed it. Afterwards, it did not happen. Wang asked for the return of the security deposit. Wang hired a lawyer to accuse Zhuang of fraudulently obtaining money. The Special District Local Court heard the case. Zhuang Jian'an denied the fraud. Shen Yuesheng was hired to submit a statement, stating that the defendant wanted to introduce Zhuang Zhongcai to be the comprador, the stated comprador security deposit was 5,000 yuan, and the fee was 2,000 yuan. The plaintiff Wang Hancai volunteered to be the deputy comprador under Zhuang Zhongcai.

Zhuang transferred 2,000 yuan to the Yicheng Company. There was a small contract that each held. Later, Yicheng decided to rent the Hanping steamship back to Yicheng due to the unstable situation. The Shanghai-Yangzhou route was opened. Wang introduced Zhuang Ruozhou to join. Wang introduced Zhuang Ruozhou to join the shareholders of the Hanping Steamship Bureau. The money was transferred to the rental of the ship. Wang also signed. Afterwards, the capital of the wheel bureau was insufficient. The defendant borrowed 2,000 yuan from Jiang Nanheng for application. Therefore, the defendant was brought into the shareholder list of the Wheel Bureau.

At the beginning of December, it was publicly agreed to hire Jiang Nanheng as the manager of the Wheel Bureau and as the chief representative. The shareholders on the letter of engagement were the defendant, Zhuang Zhongcai, Zhuang Ruozhou, and Wang Hancai. The lawyer certified it. Later, the Hanping Wheel Bureau's business declined. The capital was depleted. The debts were heavy. Yicheng had insufficient rent. The ship was taken back at the end of April. The Wheel Bureau went out of business. The defendant asked the lawyer to gather everyone, but Zhuang Zhongcai and Zhuang Ruozhou were absent. Wang Hancai claimed to not be a shareholder. The defendant filed a lawsuit and was accused of fraud. The evidence showed that Wang had signed his name on the letter of engagement. If there was any kind of fraud, the shareholder would have a joint behavior. The facts are not true. As for Wang, he paid 2,000 yuan which had become the company's rent, then the responsibility had been fulfilled.

It is obvious that the claims are false. Therefore, the defendant is not guilty of fraud. The defendant filed a civil suit. Please dismiss the accusation. The hearing was scheduled to continue on the day before yesterday, but due to the time, Judge Feng adjourned the case for another hearing.

Adding the Cause of Death to Coffin Transport Guarantees 113

Yesterday, the Shanghai Special Municipality Public Security Bureau approved an official letter from the Health Bureau, referring to an order from the Ministry of Health and a request from the Guangdong Special Municipality Government to ban coffin transport. It directed that when issuing coffin transport permits, attention should be paid to the cause of death of the deceased. If the deceased died of an epidemic disease, the Regulations on the Prevention of Infectious Diseases should be followed. The letter was recorded and communicated for investigation. After approving the letter, Director Yuan stated that coffin transport for reburial mostly involves people of non-local origin. They often place the deceased in temporary sheds after death, and by the time they are transported back to their hometown for burial, the bodies have often already decomposed. If attention is only paid to the cause of death when applying for permits, it would be too late and would not fully align with the original intention of epidemic prevention. According to Articles 13 and 14 of the Regulations on the Prevention of Infectious Diseases, the bodies of those who died of epidemic diseases must be disinfected, placed in coffins within 24 hours, and buried in a location more than three *li* away from the city center, at a depth of more than seven *chi*. Therefore, attention should be paid to investigating the cause of death when reporting the death. If there are any doubts, the relevant district office should notify the Health Bureau at any time to dispatch personnel for joint handling. However, the inspection time should be within 24 hours after death, as corpses that have been exposed for too long are prone to spreading infection, and identification would also be greatly affected. In addition to adding the cause of death to the current coffin transport guarantee form and ordering all district offices to supervise household registration police to handle it diligently, a reply was sent to the Health Bureau yesterday for their information.

Shi Zijian Fails to Pay Alimony 114

Ex-wife Hires Lawyer to Sue for Recovery

The woman Shi Shen, also known as Shen Xiaomei, hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the court, accusing her husband Shi Zijian of abandonment and requesting a divorce and the recovery of alimony. However, after the judgment, Shi has resisted and refused to comply. The lawyer representing Shen filed a case the day before yesterday, requesting prompt enforcement, stating that Shen and her daughter are now in extreme poverty and rely on this money to survive. They requested that the defendant be brought to court and severely punished to deter cunning behavior. Judge Zhu approved the order to summon the defendant to court for enforcement.

Brawl in a Teahouse on Hongqiao Road 115

Seeking a Tea Brewing Dispute, Gathering Crowds for a Brawl

Multiple Injuries, Lives in Danger

Gao Ali, a 33-year-old from Yancheng, opened the Fuxing Teahouse in a bungalow without a number (the house number was demolished by the British Municipal Council last year when they overstepped their boundaries) on the west side of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway on Hongqiao Road, West Shanghai. Recently, business has been slow, so he hired blind storytellers in the evening to maintain business. On the evening before last (the 31st), at approximately 9:40 PM, Lü Shengfu, the brother-in-law of Deng Genhua, a man from Jintan who runs the Tongxing Mantou Shop next door, came to listen to the storytelling. Gao immediately went forward to greet him and arrange a seat. However, Lü did not want to brew tea, which led to a dispute. Deng heard about it and gathered workers from a nearby laundry shop, armed with iron pipes, to reason with Gao. Seeing the unfavorable situation, Gao also sought assistance from the Eastern Province Milk Shed. Neither side would back down, and the scene became chaotic, with loud noises and teapots and tables being smashed. As a result, six people were injured, including Deng's brother-in-law, Fu Honglai, a 22-year-old from Jintan, who was seriously injured; Deng's wife, Ms. Fu, who suffered minor arm injuries; Gao Ali's brother, Gao Ruhong, 40 years old, seriously injured; Gao's nephew, Gao Wenxiu, 18 years old, seriously injured, revived after appearing to be dead; a teahouse customer, Zhang Chenggen, 36 years old from Changzhou, suffered head injuries; and Fang Kaoshan, 42 years old from Changzhou, suffered injuries to his head and arms. After the patrol officer Zhang Xiangrui of the local police station heard the alarm, he immediately dispatched police officers to the scene and brought Gao Ali, Deng Genhua, Deng's wife Ms. Fu, and Lü Shengfu back to the station. The others fled. Fu Honglai, Gao Ruhong, and Gao Wenxiu, who were seriously injured, were taken by car to the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road for treatment. Due to internal injuries, their lives may not be saved. Director Xu, considering the case involved a brawl, submitted a document to the local court yesterday morning for investigation.

Suspecting Wife of Infidelity, Jumps into River 116

The evening before last at approximately 9:00 PM, a middle-aged man with a sorrowful expression was seen pacing back and forth along the Suzhou Creek in Zhabei for a long time. Ren Kuochen, the guard officer of the 27th post in the Fourth District, suspected his behavior and followed him closely. After a while, the man jumped into the river and drifted away. The guard officer was extremely alarmed and called for the help of local boatmen to rescue him. He was successfully saved and taken to the police station. He confessed that his name was Wang Yongbiao, from Shaoxing, 40 years old, a carpenter living at No. 43 Chongde Lane, Xinmin Road. He had been married to his wife, Ms. Zhong, for five years, and initially they were happy. However, recently she had become restless and had an affair with someone. He had repeatedly warned her, but she did not change. He had lost all face, and knowing that he was unable to control her, he could not bear his wife engaging in such shameless behavior. He was filled with anger and jumped into the river to kill himself. The police chief immediately ordered the police to summon Ms. Zhong, who stated that she was 34 years old and her previous husband had passed away seven years ago. Unable to make a living, she became involved with Wang. A few days ago, she went to visit a younger female friend, but Wang suspected that she was doing improper things outside. In fact, she was quite well-behaved. The police chief, based on the confessions, stated that since they had lived together for many years, there was no need for emotional disputes. Wang Yongbiao's attempt to take his own life without reason was reckless and they should both go home and reconcile.

Tongren Hospital Issues Annual Report 127

63rd Session

The 63rd report of Tongren Hospital has recently been issued. The number of inpatients at the hospital last year increased compared to the previous year, totaling 2,719. 2,342 patients were cured and discharged. 1,271 surgeries were performed, with October being the busiest month, totaling 131 surgeries. The cost of providing for each inpatient is approximately 1.76 yuan per day. The average length of stay for each inpatient is 20.9 days, as most of those who come to the hospital for treatment have serious illnesses, so they inevitably stay in the hospital for a longer period. There were a total of 98,895 outpatient visits, an increase of 13,112 visits compared to last year. Among them, injuries caused by traffic accidents accounted for 5,900 visits, and those who took poison accounted for 547 visits, most of whom were trying to commit suicide. The total revenue for the year was 130,993 taels, with donations accounting for half of the revenue, totaling 61,065 taels. The total expenditure was 125,836 taels. The hospital's attached nursing training school usually has 50 students throughout the year. Seven students graduated last winter.

Preparatory Meeting for Dredging the Sanlintang Canal 130

The Sanlintang Canal in Pudong is an important canal in the county. Recently, due to gradual siltation, local people have discussed dredging it. However, due to insufficient funds, it has been delayed. However, the canal is of great importance to farmland irrigation and navigation. The County Construction Bureau, together with the Fourth District Office, initiated preparations for dredging. Yesterday, the first preparatory meeting was held at the District Office. County Magistrate Yan was unable to attend due to other matters and delegated Director Wu of the Construction Bureau to represent him. More than 50 people attended. Bi Huan chaired the meeting and conducted the ceremony. The chairman reported on the situation last year, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Regarding the scope of the dredging area of the Sanlintang Canal, it was resolved to proceed according to the old plan, from the Huangpu River in the west to the end of the Sanlintang Canal in the east, turning south to Guanyintang in Chen Village. At the same time, the Xin Jing Canal should also be dredged and the Qian Shan Huangpu should be cleared. (2) Regarding how to raise dredging funds, it was resolved: (A) To continue to use the method of collecting funds from farmland, and the association will separately submit requests to the County Government and the Construction Bureau, and forward them to the Financial and Construction Departments for review and approval. (B) The association will jointly raise funds from shops with the Commercial and Industrial Association. (4) Regarding the appointment of preparatory committee members, it was resolved to appoint Wu Wenhua, Bi Huan, Kang Qiang, Tang Luqiao, and 21 others as preparatory committee members, and to appoint Bi Huan as the chairman of the committee. (5) Regarding whether to stipulate the date for on-site inspection, it was resolved to schedule the on-site inspection for June 21st. (6) Regarding scheduling the next meeting, it was scheduled for July 11th.

Zhang Xianqing Reports on the Situation in Shaanxi for Disaster Relief 133

Zhang Xianqing, Director of the Shaanxi Disaster Relief of the Chinese Jishanghui, arrived in Shaanxi on April 4 and sent a letter stating that the gentlemen Zhu Ziqiao in Tianjin initiated an emergency relief effort to save lives with three yuan per person, which should have been advertised in the newspapers. The progress of the Shaanxi disaster relief is described as follows: (1) On the way through Shaanxian County in Henan, the county's porridge factory needed grain, and Zhu Ziqiao was entrusted to purchase 7,000 yuan of millet, approximately 700 *shi*, which has been delivered to the factory. (2) Shaanxian County, Xin'an, and Mianchi are lacking seeds. 20,000 yuan worth of seeds were co-organized with Huisheng Society and allocated to Zhu Ziqiao to transport and distribute. (3) The Shaanxi Disaster Relief Association sent a telegram regarding immigration. If immigrants are sent, please telegraph and vehicles will be sent to Shaanxi to pick them up. (4) The two disaster relief shelters in Xi'an previously housed several thousand people. Those who have no homes still need to be cared for until after the autumn and then dispersed. (5) The Xianyang disaster relief shelter for children previously housed over 400 children. The director of the shelter requested an extension of care and an increase in funding. He was allowed to check and then a decision would be made. (6) The Wugong disaster relief shelter for children has housed over 300 children and still needs to be provided for. (7) There are too many difficult problems in this disaster relief effort in Shaanxi. It is difficult to describe them all in writing. There are many people in the disaster area who are on the verge of death. Our association can only do its best to save as many people as possible. We hope that kind people at home and colleagues in Shanghai will prepare to provide relief to avoid widespread starvation.

Zhao Shouheng's Conversation 134

A reporter from the New Shanghai News Agency encountered Zhao Shouheng, Director of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau, yesterday and inquired about matters concerning the reorganization of the bureau's affairs. Director Zhao stated that the report published the other day, "Discussion on the Reorganization of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau," contained considerable misunderstandings. Furthermore, his surname "Shouheng" was mistaken for "Zhao Chuanyu" (note: the former Shanghai director). Moreover, the item about dismissing office staff, claiming that "Zhao is going to replace almost all personnel within the bureau, from section chiefs to tea servers," is even further from the truth. Shouheng initially led the Suzhou Telephone Bureau and was transferred by order to exchange positions with the former Director Zhao Chuanyu. All the previous personnel, except for a portion who went to Suzhou to work with the former director, remain in their positions. Only a few idle and redundant staff members were slightly reduced to save expenses. As for the branch offices, such as Jiangwan, Nanxiang, and the two Zhabei branch offices, due to the simplicity of their affairs, there was no need to add office staff, so they were also appropriately reduced, and their duties were taken over by the heads of the respective branch offices. Other branch offices with more complex affairs remained as before. It was also said that each bureau has two to three hundred telephone lines. According to the Shanghai Bureau's current count, there are a total of two thousand two hundred and two lines: 1,739 lines in the main bureau, 394 in Zhabei, 39 in Jiangwan, 19 in Nanxiang, and 11 in Wusong. As for promoting women's lives, according to the facts, this is also largely inaccurate. This bureau has always employed female operators. In addition, the engineering department employs a few female clerks, all of whom have been employed by previous administrations and have not been changed. Shouheng also has no plans to employ female staff as heads of the treasury department or office staff in the document department. Director Zhao also stated that his bureau had received an order from the ministry to set up a refresher school for operators and technicians. While Shouheng was in charge of the Suzhou Bureau, he made efforts to manage this matter and achieved considerable results. This time, upon arriving in Shanghai, he also intends to actively reorganize, but due to the limited address of this bureau, there is currently no suitable location to use as a classroom. He is currently looking for a solution. In addition, plans are being made to find suitable locations for establishing employee clubs, reading rooms, and ball courts for female operators, which will be gradually implemented. As for the matter of reorganizing telephone operations and saving excessive expenses, Shouheng was determined to do so from the beginning of his term. He hopes to implement the ministry's orders to the best of his ability within the possible scope. However, the newspaper's claim of establishing a driver's school is a misunderstanding. Although Shouheng is constantly reorganizing the bureau's affairs, mistakes are inevitable. He hopes that the gentlemen of the press will provide guidance at any time.

Beggar Dies on the Road 135

Yesterday morning at about 8:00 AM, on the sidewalk at the entrance of Lane 3, Ruifu Lane, Xizilaihuo Street, in the French Concession, a person resembling a beggar suddenly collapsed and died. He was about forty years old, his clothes were torn and ragged. A Chinese patrolman noticed this and immediately returned to the police station to report. After receiving the report, the head of the police station ordered the body to be sent to the Tongren Fuyuantang funeral home for coffining and burial.

"Ciyou Monthly" Second Issue Published 138

The second issue of the "Ciyou Monthly," founded by the China Child Welfare Association, was published the day before yesterday. This issue focuses on the issue of child protection and is specially themed the "Child Protection Issue." The front of the volume features inscriptions by Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Special Municipal Government Social Bureau, and Mr. Li Xiaobai, Professor of Chinese Studies at the China Vocational School, as well as several copperplate printed photos. The most outstanding essays include Mr. Wu Weide's "The Issue of Child Protection," Mr. Chen Zhengfan's "The International Labor Bureau and Child Protection," Lawyer Wang Yaotang's "Suggestions on the Establishment of a Children's Court," Ms. Li Guanfang's "The Significance of the Young Motherhood Corps," Mr. Wang Guanyi's "The Procedures of Child Welfare Work," and Mr. Wang Zhion's "Miserable Slaves of the Autocratic Era." All are important and valuable works. There are many association news items, briefly outlining the recent projects undertaken by the association. The colorful cover painting is by the famous Shanghai artist Feng Zikai and is very beautiful. In order to make the publication accessible to a wider society, the association has set an unusually low price.

Recent News on the Reorganization of the Tobacco Exchange Industry Groups 139

Since the Shanghai Special Municipality Tobacco Exchange Industry Group Reorganization Committee sent personnel to various roads in the Chinese and Concession areas to distribute door-to-door price lists and encourage colleagues to fill out voluntary registration forms, abide by the regulations, eliminate the practice of hanging signs to sell at low prices, and achieve uniformity, the situation is about to be unified. Currently, due to the sudden increase in the price of cigarettes and soaps and the daily decline in foreign prices, Xu Yunxiang and Zhang Songji, members of the Reorganization Committee in the southern district, have repeatedly received requests from various members to convene a meeting to re-determine prices in order to maintain capital and benefit livelihoods. It is reported that the association will convene a meeting of the Reorganization Committee at 3:00 PM this Wednesday to discuss the following important proposals: (1) Receiving a letter from the Commercial Reorganization Association on June 21, convening a representative assembly of the industry guild, should elect the number of representatives to attend and submit representative fees; (2) Schedule elections, submit them to higher-level agencies for filing and approval, and request them to send personnel to supervise and guide the establishment; (3) Issue membership certificates to registered members for identification; (4) For those who disrupt the retail price, submit reports to various higher-level agencies for public judgment and punishment.

The Eight-Day Session is Too Long 143

It is Difficult to Concentrate on the Competition

Change to Four Days and Cancel the Public Competition

This newspaper's Tokyo dispatch dated the 1st: After the closing of the Far Eastern Games, public opinion is that the eight-day session seems too long. It is better to change it to four days, so that we can concentrate our minds and energy to determine the outcome, and not be tired from being too long. Public performances often have temporary non-participants, which is enough to devalue the spirit of the conference. Therefore, public opinion may cancel it in the future.

Ticket Revenue is 120,000 144

520,000 Spectators in Eight Days

This newspaper's Tokyo dispatch dated the 1st: During the eight days of this conference, except for a rain shower, the weather was clear, so the audience was extraordinarily large. According to a survey by the Japanese Sports Association, the number of spectators in eight days exceeded 520,000, and the ticket revenue reached 120,000 yen. The daily average is about 60,000 people, with the athletics field being the most popular.

The Cost of Meals for Athletes is 10,000 Yuan 145

Our Country Spent 5,500

This newspaper's Tokyo dispatch dated the 1st: The cost of accommodation and meals used by the participating countries is as follows: China 5,500 yuan, the Philippines 4,600 yuan, and India 334 yuan, totaling about 10,000 yen.

Infighting in the Japanese Sports World 146

The Japan Association of Athletics is About to Leave the Association of Advancement

This newspaper's Tokyo dispatch dated the 1st: Judging from the phenomenon, the Japan Association of Athletics seems to be withdrawing from the Japan Sports Association after the completion of the Far Eastern Games, because of the disagreement on the issue of adopting world rules for the 9th Games. The Federation has convened a meeting of staff to discuss everything. Because it was a secret meeting, the details are not yet known. However, it is heard that the members are divided into two factions, one advocating separation and the other advocating major changes in the personnel of the Japan Sports Association. According to the news from those who advocate separation, the International Student Games will be held in Darmstadt, Germany, so the Federation will probably separate from the Association. This matter is now very much concerned by the Japanese sports world.

Shortcomings in Japanese Management 147

This newspaper's Tokyo dispatch dated the 1st:

At each conference, the host country is always criticized, but not as much as this time in Japan. Because Japan is very confident in track and field and swimming, there is no act of causing disputes. However, for the three items of basketball, football, and volleyball, means were used, and other countries' athletes were treated with partiality. Japan-style will use inexperience or ignorance of the rules as an excuse, but the referee does not follow the rules, resulting in Japanese athletes using tricks, and the other party often protests, which hinders international friendship. This is in fact against the purpose of the conference to connect feelings. For example, before the opening of the conference, there were disagreements within the organization regarding the adoption of world rules. Externally, there were negotiations on not including the eulogy of our foreign minister Wang and the Indian flag not being available. If Japan wants not to reduce the spirit of the future conference, this kind of action must be eliminated. As for the transmission of news between staff members, it can also be organized. The propaganda committee members cannot forecast the time for each competition, which makes it inconvenient for participants and spectators. As for other shortcomings, it is difficult to describe in detail. In short, Japan cannot escape people's blame, because it cannot treat people sincerely, and the referee does not follow the rules and is also biased. The end result is that disputes often arise, damaging international friendship, leaving a permanent regret in sports.

China-Japan Football War

The Situation When Our Country's Forward Chen Guangyao Kicked Japan's Second Goal

Japanese Female Students Ask for Autographs 148

} Demanding Philippine Athletes }

Police Investigated a Total of Sixty-Four People

Educational Issues That Arise Should Be Considered

This newspaper's Tokyo dispatch dated the 1st: During the Far Eastern Games, many Japanese female students asked Philippine athletes for autographs. According to a survey by the Japanese police, there were 64 people, which is an educational issue that should be considered and has attracted attention from all sides.

Anecdotes from the Venue 149

(Qu from Tokyo)

Athletes Are Busy Signing Autographs

The Japanese worship athletes, especially women. During this conference, whenever athletes left the competition venue, they were surrounded by a large number of Japanese young female students, who took out their exquisite small notebooks to ask the athletes to sign their names as souvenirs. As a result, the lounge of the athletes' lodging and the corners and intersections nearby were all crowded with groups of women, hindering traffic. The staff in charge of organizing the venue posted a large advertisement saying [Athletes Refuse to Sign], but the trend of signing autographs has not diminished at all.

The Upright Wu Meixian 150

The trend of signing autographs is rampant, and the handiwork of female athletes is even more precious. Our country's female athletes are most admired by the crowd in the conference, and there are even more people asking them to sign their names. Ms. Wu Meixian believes that this kind of action is an elegant thing if it is done occasionally, but it is a bit boring if it is disturbed for many days. Therefore, she generally refuses. Originally, signing autographs is one of the means of international communication in the conference. In order to leave a good impression, it seems that one should not refuse people too strictly, and Ms. Wu's vigorous action may be too upright.

The Sun Family, Buried Talents 151

Sun Guiyun, our nation's female athlete admired by tens of thousands, made her first appearance on the 27th. We had high expectations for her. However, in the 100-meter selection, the starter (Sgauter) repeatedly made things difficult for her, nitpicking excessively, leading Ms. Sun to withdraw. In the women's 400-meter relay race, Ms. Sun ran the final leg, but due to the late handoffs by the first two runners, even though Ms. Sun's speed surpassed that of the Japanese final runner, the initial deficit was too large, and she did not succeed.

Vendors Good at Speculation 152

Around 3 PM on the 27th, during the intense track and field competitions, the sky suddenly clouded over and it began to rain. The audience was greatly troubled, when suddenly vendors transported a large batch of oiled paper umbrellas to the site, hawking them around. The audience eagerly bought them, not caring about the high prices. The vendors made ten times their profit in an instant. The Japanese people's skill in speculation can be seen here.

Detailed Records of the 9th Far Eastern Games (3) 153

First China-Japan Basketball Game

(Xu Minhun)

Thirty-Nine to Twenty-Four... Japan Wins Over China

(Tokyo Correspondence) All ball games, except for tennis, are using a double round-robin system (meaning each team plays against the other teams twice). The first game was between China and Japan, held at 7:45 PM on May 24th at the newly built Meiji Jingu basketball and volleyball court. The result was a great surprise to us. A special record of the new Far Eastern Games is noted as follows:

(1) The Game Situation 154

At the sound of the mobilization order, the athletes from both sides competed on the field. In less than two minutes, the Chinese team was penalized twice. Japan's Ohashi and Oda scored two points through free throws. Under the strict surveillance of the referees and inspectors, the Chinese team could not move freely, and the morale of the team was flustered. Japan's Nomura seized the opportunity to attack from afar and scored. In less than three minutes, the score was 4-0. The five Chinese players showed their might. Tang and Yao passed quickly and returned a goal. Shortly after, Yao scored two more points with a long shot. At this point, both teams had 4 points. The Chinese team then changed its plan, using long shots to catch up with Japan. However, Japan's Ohashi and Ouchi each made a free throw, and the score became tied again. Tang was agile and shot quickly, adding to the Chinese record. However, Tanaka's long shot was not weak either, and both teams competed fiercely. At the 18th minute, the scoreboard showed 13-12, with Japan in the lead. In the last minute, Ueda also scored with a long shot. The result of the first half was 15-12, with Japan winning. During the break, the spectators were worried for the Chinese team. However, the instructor and the players believed that Japan was not their opponent. They thought that the reason they were able to gain an advantage was just due to the luck of the long shots. They believed that the Chinese team would eventually win. However, after the break, in less than a minute, Japan's Ueda and Ohashi scored two consecutive goals. China's Little Yao returned a goal. Japan's Ohashi scored two more points with a long shot, making the score 21-14. At this time, China's Tang scored a free throw, and Wei scored a goal with a long shot. The score was close again, and the atmosphere of the entire court was tense. The Japanese team invigorated their spirit, and Ueda used long shots to score two more goals. Japan's Kobayashi also used a long shot, but missed. Ohashi missed a free throw. However, by the 13th minute of the second half, the score difference was already 12 points. The Chinese spectators thought that the situation was hopeless. However, the Chinese team still fought with all their might. Li Guoshen scored two points with a long shot. Liu Zhongjiang received a long pass from his teammate and shot from the left side of the basket, scoring one point. At this time, the scoreboard showed 30-22, and the Chinese supporters cheered for them. The Japanese team announced tightened security in their area, and the Chinese team could not approach. They then deployed new force Lu Zongen into the game, who made repeated long shots, but missed. Instead, the Japanese took advantage of the opportunity to attack. The Chinese army ordered a quick return to defense, but it was too late. In the last few minutes, the Japanese team, either with long shots or short passes, scored 8 points in a row, all by Ueda, and also scored a free throw. China's Lu Jun rushed forward and scored two points with a long shot. At this time, the Chinese team had good coordination and quick passing, but time was up. The gun sounded, and the game ended. The result was 39-24, with Japan winning.

(2) General Review of the Game 155

The Japanese have never paid much attention to basketball, but since returning from the last time, they have actively promoted it to wipe out the shame of the past Far Eastern Games. The progress of the players was beyond our expectations. The reason they were able to win against our team can be summarized as fast and accurate shooting and passing. Most of their points were from long shots. All the team members were able to endure hardship and were never tired from beginning to end. However, in terms of formation, they were still immature. I predict that in the future Far Eastern Games, they will be a major concern for China and the Philippines. The Chinese team is a well-trained team with a lot of experience and no opponent in the country. They looked down on everything and thought that basketball in a small, nameless island nation was not worth fearing. They were too confident. As the saying goes, "Humility brings benefit, complacency invites loss," which can be a warning for the Chinese basketball team. After losing the game, they complained about the umpires, which is not the attitude a sportsman should have. However, people's hearts are different, and the strictness, accuracy, wisdom, honesty, and cunning of the umpires are also not uniform. Our team has a lot of experience, but there is still something lacking, namely, the attitude towards the umpires. The umpires have different personalities, qualities, knowledge, and experiences. During normal practice, players should eliminate all illegal and bad habits, even if there are suspicious points. Do not use the weaknesses of the umpires and develop bad habits. Even if the umpire has shallow knowledge, we must follow the rules. If there are any who are deliberately biased, do not argue with them. Even if you are wrongly penalized several times, you must remain calm and not be anxious. Under the watchful eyes of the public, those with a little conscience will not dare to openly cheat. Even if they do, public opinion will prevail, and you will still be honorable even if you lose. Otherwise, even if you argue and get angry, it will not only not help, but also cause psychological, technical, and coordination stimulation to the players, making it impossible to perform to their full potential. Often, strong teams lose to weak teams because they are fighting against the opposing team on one hand and against the umpires on the other. If this is the case, there are few who do not lose. The organizers should negotiate with them appropriately. Sometimes, there is no better option than to deal with them as they are.

In terms of technique, the Chinese team used a five-man zone defense. Although this defense is strict, there are several ways to break it. The Japanese team knew our situation well and had planned to break our defense with long shots. If you look at the record, most of the points scored by the Japanese were from long shots, which shows this. The Chinese team members were stable, but they were too slow in holding the ball, passing, and shooting, and often missed opportunities because of this. They also passed the ball too much, and had to pass the ball to the basket before shooting. The Japanese were agile and often stole the ball, making it impossible to get close to the basket. Therefore, they had very few opportunities to shoot. They had no choice but to change their plan and use long shots, but they had not practiced this much and were often inaccurate, so they lost more than they gained. Some team members lacked self-control, and were distracted by the umpires' fouls and the spectators' scolding. If a teammate or they themselves made a mistake, they would be anxious and show it in their actions. These are all reasons for our team's failure.

Women's Singles China vs. Philippines 158

First Match: Li Xinghua Wins Against Philippines' Caliaga

Second Match: Mrs. Afu Wins Against China's Li Mudan

First Match: China's Li Xinghua defeated Philippines' Ms. Caliaga 6-1, 6-1. Just as the first men's match ended, the well-known Li sisters of China appeared. Ms. Li served first, winning two sets in a row. Ms. Caliaga tried to catch up and won one set, but her skills were not refined, and her serves often failed. Ms. Xinghua was able to conserve her energy and lost four sets in a row. Ms. Li then won the first set 6-1. Starting from the second set, Ms. Li's momentum increased, winning the first game with a score of four to two. Then, in a long rally, Ms. Caliaga won one game, which was her last win of the day. After that, Ms. Li cruised to victory, winning 6-1.

Second Match: Philippines' Mrs. Afu (MRF Ochoa) defeated China's Li Mudan 6-2, 5-7, 6-1. The second women's match was a fierce battle, and one of the most exciting scenes in today's women's competition. Li started the serve and was immediately at a disadvantage, losing a total of five games. Mrs. Afu had the momentum to continue, but in the sixth and seventh games, Mudan suddenly regained her spirit and her shots were effective, giving the opponent no chance to win. The audience thought the situation had changed, and China was about to turn the tide, but Mrs. Afu stepped up her efforts and won two consecutive games, winning the first set 6-2. The battle in the second set was even more intense. Mudan received a lot of cheers, and her performance was indeed strong, but she could not maintain it and ultimately lost in the third set. Initially, each won one game, and then each won two consecutive games, making the score 2-3. Mrs. Afu advanced bravely in the seventh and eighth games, gaining a 5-3 lead. Ms. Li rushed to catch up, and as a result of the bloody battle, recovered the situation with a score of 7-5, winning the second set. This winning streak, which turned defeat into victory, terrified the Philippine athlete. Mrs. Afu looked tired and moved slowly, while Mudan ran quickly to the left and right, the ball arrived where she did, and she had a smile on her face, as if she was confident. Unexpectedly, heaven did not help her. Ms. Li, after her brave fight, was inevitably negligent and was taken advantage of by the opponent. The third set of the final began, and she lost four games in a row. Although she cheered herself up and won the fifth game, it was too late to save the situation, and she lost two more games, finally losing 1-6.

Overall, the performance of the Japanese athletes Sato and Bui was indeed strong. There should be no problem beating the Philippines. In the future, they will have a bloody battle with our Lin and Qiu. It is hard to predict who will win. On the women's side, the two Lis are strong players, and Philippines' Mrs. Afu is also a strong opponent. The victory or defeat of the China-Philippines women's team may be decided in tomorrow's doubles match. However, the Japanese women's athletes are strong, and even if we beat the Philippines, we still need to make a special effort. In terms of the two Li's skills, Ms. Xinghua's opponent was weaker, so both games were very easy. Her serve was accurate and powerful. Ms. Mudan's performance was very good, and she was honorable even in defeat. Her ball showed special effort. However, she was too conservative and rarely attacked, allowing the enemy to conserve energy. She also used the trick of feinting to the east and attacking the west to score points. Ms. Mudan's skill in striking the ball was quite impressive, and this was how she won the sixth and seventh games of the first set. If she could use it more often when she has a good opportunity, Mrs. Afu's defeat would be no problem. I wonder if Miss Li would agree.

Important News

Soviet Church Passes First Step in Implementing Trial Free Education 164

The second meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Compulsory Education Committee was held at 3:00 PM on May 29th. Attendees included Xie Bing, Zhu Jingnong, Ye Chucang, Chen Shunian, Chen Hexian, Yang Naikang, Huang Shaohong, Duan Yuhua. The chairman was Chen Hexian, and the recorder was Huang Shaohong. The meeting began as scheduled.

Reported Matters: The chairman reported on the state of compulsory education in various counties in Jiangsu. Matters for Discussion: 1. Amendment of the Jiangsu Provincial Compulsory Education Experimental Zone Plan. Resolutions: (1) The plan was amended and passed. (2) A detailed budget will be prepared by the Department of Education for the 19th year, limited to 150,000 yuan. (3) Wu Zhihui, Ye Chucang, and Chen Shunian were publicly recommended to discuss the funding. 2. Plan to establish [separate] and [centralized] normal schools. Resolution: This case was referred to the three members Zhu, Xu, and Xie for review, and the Department of Agriculture and Mining was requested to appoint personnel from agricultural institutions to participate. 3. First step in implementing trial compulsory education. Resolution: Passed. The meeting adjourned at 5:15 PM.

First Step in Implementing Trial Compulsory Education (Yang Naikang) The preliminary plan for implementing compulsory education at this National Education Conference has already been decided under the goal item: [Children who cannot continue to study for four years may be allowed to flexibly adjust their study period by using supplementary schools or self-study systems to make up for the compulsory education they should receive.] This is a consideration for impoverished children. We, on the other hand, are considering the perspective of setting up schools. Given the current economic capacity and teacher situation in each county, it is practically impossible to ensure that all school-age children can attend primary school. If we ask them to wait until the provincial and county funds are sufficient and the teachers are ready, then they will have been delayed for quite some time and will suffer a great loss.

Therefore, we should now adopt a [humble and down-to-earth] attitude to ensure that these out-of-school children can quickly have the opportunity to study. In 1852, Massachusetts first promulgated a compulsory education system, stipulating that children aged eight to fourteen must attend school for twelve weeks each year. This was later promoted to other states. By 1898, 22 states had a compulsory education system. The implementation of compulsory education nationwide was not completed until 1919. Japan promulgated an education system in the fifth year of Meiji, stipulating that a primary school district should be established in areas with a population of more than 600, and all children over the age of six, regardless of gender, must be sent to school. Initially, they also stipulated that they must attend school for four months each year, with a completion period of sixteen months, and then advance to a three-year simplified course. Now it has been set at six years. Looking at the past history of compulsory education in the United States and Japan, their compulsory education was also very simple at first. It was not until the country's economy was sufficient that it became what it is today. Therefore, we do not need to rush to imitate their current situation. We should start by doing what they did before.

In my personal opinion, according to the meaning of the flexible measures resolved at this National Education Conference, we should first try to run a two-hour primary school, recruiting children around ten years old who cannot fully attend formal primary school, and force them to study for two hours every day. The content of the courses taught should be less than that of the current primary school. It is enough to have a few major subjects. Assuming that 500 hours (30,000 minutes) are taught each year, 1,500 hours (90,000 minutes) will be considered compulsory education.

In this way, assuming that each teacher teaches for eight hours a day, each classroom can rotate to receive four levels of children. Wouldn't one teacher be able to be used as four people, one classroom as four classrooms, and one level of funding as four levels? This is the most economical method.

This method is not a step backward. It is because there are too many out-of-school children now. For example, when you encounter people who are starving every day, the relief workers do not even give rice soup because the food is insufficient. They must wait until the rice is sufficient before letting them eat their fill. I'm afraid they would have starved to death long ago. Therefore, we should now use the [method of feeding rice soup to temporarily maintain their lives, gradually increasing the number of years and enriching the content step by step from simple to complex. There is no need to wait until the funding and teachers are sufficient before running the schools.

If you think this principle can be passed, I would like to propose a few measures to try out in a few designated counties in Jiangsu, or to designate a few places in a certain county to try out, and at the same time, we should also stipulate a few simple compulsory school attendance measures to test it.

Jiangsu Education Department Disapproves Huaiyin's Examination for Education Bureau Director 167

Feng Zanyuan, the Director of the Education Bureau of Huaiyin County, resigned. The County Magistrate of the county, Xu Jiaqing, recommended as many as seven people to succeed him. The Jiangsu Education Department, considering this incompatible with the County Organization Law, instructed the magistrate to recommend candidates according to the regulations. The magistrate then suggested holding an examination in the county to determine the order of recommendation, citing the large number of hopefuls. The Department of Education, upon hearing this, considered it increasingly bizarre and in violation of regulations, and has issued an order rejecting the proposal.

Economist Dr. Li Quanshi has recently compiled his four treatises on Consumption, Production, Exchange, and Distribution into a major volume entitled "Principles of Economics," published and distributed by the Southeast Bookstore at 90 Hart Road in this city. Finance: The Week's Gold Premium Rose 22.7 Taels 176

Breaking New Records

Highest Peak at 544.9 Taels

Huge Fluctuations Throughout the Week: The volatility of the gold premium in the past week was particularly intense, with daily fluctuations of around ten taels. It almost broke through the 540-tael mark. Although rumors about the silver tax issue were not as prevalent as in the previous week, they were still occasionally raised, causing a temporary setback. The severe contraction of Da Tiao (silver futures) and foreign exchange was truly rare, leading to repeated new records. The bewilderment in the minds of industry professionals and the disarray of their decision-making were unprecedented, with no sense of certainty. It was entirely influenced by the atmosphere. The week began with a surge to a peak, followed by turbulent storms and various rumors, which briefly broke the 520-tael mark, plummeting to 518.3 taels. Subsequently, it soared again, almost reaching unprecedented heights, unexpectedly reaching a new historical peak of 544.9 taels. By the weekend, the market was relatively stable, but the underlying upward trend remained. The exchange rate, however, did not move in tandem with the gold price at the beginning of the week, but by the weekend, the arbitrage seemed to narrow slightly, not as far apart as before. Yet, the gold price was still lower than the quoted exchange rate by as much as 50 to 60 taels. As a result, the gold price continued to rise compared to the previous week. Here is a detailed account of the events of the week from May 26th to May 31st:

A Weekly Review of 26.6 Taels: On Monday (May 26th), the English and American silver prices declined, and foreign exchange rates contracted in four rounds, totaling three levels. The gold market continued to rise, with a daily fluctuation of over nine taels. However, this was in contrast to the exchange rate market, which only rose by six or seven taels. The day opened at 521.5 taels, with a maximum of 529.4 mace (a unit of weight) and a closing price of 525.7 mace in the afternoon. The next day, although both Da Tiao and exchange rates contracted, major speculators were selling off, leading to a chaotic market situation with dangerous waves. There were fluctuations of over ten taels, with initial strength followed by weakness. In the afternoon, it fell to 518.3 taels, coupled with a sharp increase in overnight interest rates, causing fear and uncertainty. By the close of the market, it was at 519.1 mace. On Wednesday, Da Tiao and silver prices remained unchanged, and the exchange rate market stabilized. However, there was internal tightness, and major speculators were buying, leading to another rise. It jumped up by 7 taels and zero mace. The next day, the market was very firm, and the exchange rate market rose sharply, with the exchange rate listing contracting by one and a half levels. However, people were still uncertain, and the price was lower by as much as 50 taels. It had broken through the 30-tael mark, reaching 36.5 taels at one point. As a result, sellers were active, totaling 30 taels and 6 taels. On Friday, the English and American silver prices contracted sharply, with the sterling falling by three levels, totaling 75, American dollars by 1.5 yuan, and Japanese gold jumping by over 4.5 points, totaling 1 tael, 2 mace, 4 fen, 3 li, 7 hao, and 5 si. The quoted price was lower by over 60 taels, which was rare. However, the chaos in the market was indescribable, with a variation of as much as 13 taels. In the morning, due to rumors of taxation, it rose slightly. Later, the waves surged, and an unprecedented price appeared, reaching 544.9 taels, breaking a new record. However, the internal market for sterling and Japanese gold was initially tight and then eased, so the arbitrage gradually approached. The closing price was more relaxed than the previous day. The gold premium closed at 538.5 taels. On the weekend of May 31st, Da Tiao was extended again, so the foreign exchange rate was also extended by one level. However, the internal market remained firm, and the gold market was relatively calm, fluctuating by only 4 taels, hovering around the 40-tael mark. There were no large transactions in the market because the banks were closed on June 1st and 2nd, so the exchange was also closed for two days. All long and short positions had to be settled. By the time the market closed at noon, it was 541.8 taels, a total increase of 22.7 taels compared to the previous Saturday (May 24th). The highest and lowest prices for these six days had a difference of 26.6 taels.

Old woman} Oh, Mr. Wang. Why don't you even look at me when you see me? Don't you recognize me?

Record of Ye Dehui's Prison · Bing 187

The Ning-Han united to eliminate the communists. The Hunan May Fourth Incident was a major turning point. Before the May Fourth Incident, there was a major prison case in Hunan that shocked people at home and abroad. That was Ye Dehui's execution. At that time, the Hunan party and government were in the hands of the so-called leftists. The provincial city had a special court dedicated to judging reactionary cases. In half a year, there were already twenty or thirty local tyrants and evil gentry who were sentenced to death. Among them, the execution of Ye Dehui was the most eye-catching. Ye Dehui's reputation was praised by some as a seed of reading in the present world, while others vilified him as a modern literary monster. On the night Ye Dehui was arrested, he was returning from the residence of a certain female performer. The arresters were the self-defense forces of the Provincial Farmers' Association. He was sent to the special court that evening and executed the next morning. Ye Dehui was well acquainted with important figures in the Wuhan National Government such as Tan Weigong. It was also heard that He Jian had also been a student of his. Being detained in prison for a long time should have led to bail. A certain member of the special court, who was also a department head of the provincial government, was Ye's student and insisted on a speedy execution. Thus, Ye was executed as a remnant of the imperial system (he had been the chairman of the Hunan Preparatory Peace Association).

Before Ye was arrested, he once said to people, "I am not an evil gentry, but a rogue gentry." "Rogue" is a term used by the people of Hunan to scold rascals, similar to what is called "gangster" in Shanghai dialect. He also joked to people, "Some people say I am a literary monster. There are no literary monsters in Hunan, only word monsters." One is Yi Yincun and the other is Cao Mengqi. Yi liked epigraphy, and his characters were said to have silver hooks and iron brushes. Cao was good at classical Chinese prose, and his characters learned from the Northern Stele and referred to the Yan style, tracing back to the seal script to form his own style. Both of them knew Ye, so Ye made this joke. Ye liked to talk about the art of the bedroom. He collected a lot of secret performance pictures and published the "Shuangmei Landscape Collection" to circulate. He once criticized Zhang Jingsheng for talking about sexual art as an amateur. He firmly believed that he was an expert.

Ye was originally from Suzhou. Because he had lived in Hunan for a long time, he became a Hunanese. There were two pockmarked gentlemen in Hunan. Since the Wuxu Reform, they had been feared by the authorities below the governor. One was Ye Pockmark and the other was Wang Pockmark. Wang Pockmark was Wang Xianqian. Both of them were the main figures in the Yijiao Collection and were difficult for the Hunan reformers of the Wuxu Reform.

Ye's courtesy name was Huanbin and his sobriquet was Xieyuan. He wrote many works that were famous at home and abroad. Many Japanese scholars also praised him. He once wrote his own birthday preface. The first sentence began with "The people of the country all say that Ye Dehui is killable." Later, he ended badly, which was probably what is called a literary prophecy.

Unprecedented Gold Mine Discovered in Taiwan 188

Autumn Water ··

According to the Japanese news agency, a very rich gold mine has recently been discovered on the island of Taiwan. The discoverer is Dr. Jisaburo Tokobori, a professor in the Engineering Department of the Tokyo Imperial University. Dr. Tokobori has been studying mineralogy for many years and has a deep understanding of it. This trip to Taiwan was an unintentional discovery of an unprecedented source of wealth for the country. His satisfaction can be imagined. The doctor recently took the specimen back to China. For a time, the government and the public were shocked and regarded it as a grand event. A reporter from a certain newspaper visited the doctor at his home and inquired about the details. It was published in the newspaper and translated for the people of the country. It should be known that although Taiwan is small in area, it has always been a barrier to our country. The story of Zheng Chenggong at the end of the Ming Dynasty should also be vaguely in our minds. I don't know that the source of profit in it is so innumerable. The country has heard of it, and it is also felt in the heart.

The gold is worth about 500 million yuan. The doctor said that the wealth of gold in Taiwan is unimaginable. It is extremely difficult for me to give an exact number at this time. However, I am confident that once excavated, the total amount will be worth at least 500 million yen. The gold mine is located within 15 miles of the eastern coast of Taiwan, away from Lun Ge Karenko. The area spans nearly 150 miles, which is also shocking.

Gold sand is available along the street. The gold mines in the area are all contained in sand and gravel and are alluvialized by water. Therefore, there are traces of it on the ground. I (the doctor himself) also picked up gold sand and gravel in rivers, mountains, and plains. After chemical tests, the gold content is extremely rich. Even on the streets of the city, this kind of gold sand can be seen from time to time. I once picked up a little stone from a small street in a small village. After returning to the test, it actually contained gold. The richness of the gold mine in Taiwan can be imagined. The so-called "gold is available everywhere" exists in Taiwan. Therefore, the gold mine in the area is extremely easy to excavate. It is not like the gold mines in North Korea and other places. Gold seedlings are not seen unless they enter a place 100 feet deep. The gold mines in Taiwan are all floating on the ground. Excavation is effortless. Traces are not seen until 120 feet below. It is a unique source of wealth in East Asia and a gold mine that has never been seen in history in the world.

True Love Tragedy ·· Electricity 189

In the American publishing industry, there is a very popular magazine called [True Story]. The materials in this book are mostly taken from the bizarre facts in society and described and narrated. Because the true facts are always very emotional and reasonable, they are more popular. The good works in this magazine often become the material for Hollywood movies. For example, the recent film [The Strange Case of Killing His Wife] was adapted from a novel in this magazine.

Regarding the shooting of films based on true events, it has been seen frequently in our country's film industry. However, whether in Europe, America, or our country, the materials for this kind of film mostly focus on love. Especially on the tragedy of love.

Like the love case between Huang Huiru and Lu Genrong before, it was a very tortuous love tragedy. Therefore, the Mingxing Film Company once filmed a movie about the love between Huang and Lu, which was very popular. The love case between Ma Zhenhua and Wang Shichang, although the plot is very simple, is indeed a love tragedy. Therefore, some people have also made it into a movie, which is also very popular.

We know that the value of tragedy lies in making people more emotional. The true tragedy, because it is emotional and reasonable, can naturally arouse the audience's sympathy. It is best to use this kind of material to make films.

Recently, our country's Mingxing Film Company has another new film called [A Red Egg]. It is also adapted from a true story. It is said that this story is very popular in Ningbo. It is about a very virtuous girl who married a man who was born with no genitals. Unfortunately, because of a red egg given to someone else's newborn child, the girl was unjustly put to death for no reason. As a result, a good family was filled with desolation and misery.

I think that in this film, the cruelty of the old ethics and the tragic circumstances of the old families can certainly be brought into play. Then, with the twists and turns of the facts and the dazzling silver, it will definitely make people feel lingering and affectionate sympathy.

Record of Double Fish in a Brief Moment ··· Jing Mengdie 190

Early summer is clear and peaceful, but there are more storms. My wife has been bored at home since she recovered from her illness. The day before yesterday, she took advantage of the sunny weather to come to Wuxi. She will take a panoramic view of the lakes and mountains from afar. I and I sipped tea in the park, in the depths of the green shade. We took a short rest and then went to Chong'an Temple in front of the temple. I wandered around at will and bought some odd bits and pieces. There are hundreds of plays and miscellaneous things gathered here, which is no different from the Xuanmiao Temple in Suzhou and the City God Temple in Changzhou. On the side of the market, there was someone selling goldfish. There were dozens of fish swimming in the clear water. All of them were red. Only two of the larger ones were dark black and golden yellow, intertwined to form a pattern. Their appearance was especially pleasing. The owner pointed to them and said, "This is the dragon breed." His intention was to be quite odd. My wife loved them so much. So I asked me to pay four small silver coins and get this pair of treasures. She was happy, as if she had obtained Xuan Yu's double rings and Fengcheng's two swords. The owner also put them in a glass bottle and tied them with colored silk. So when we walked, we took turns carrying them. When we sat, we placed them quietly on the table and enjoyed watching them sip green algae and go up and down in the waves. That night, we stayed at the hotel. She said that she would take them back to her hometown tomorrow to break the loneliness of the empty boudoir. When we explored them the next morning, they were all stiff. My wife was shocked and did not expect it. We bitterly explored the cause of their illness. I smiled and said, "Let's not talk about other things for the time being. How much is the capacity of this small bottle? They have lost all their freedom, so that heroes have no place to use their weapons, and they are as cramped as horses under a carriage. I knew they wouldn't last long. I just wanted to take pleasure in your intentions for a while." My wife frowned and said, "In that case, they were originally lively mandarin ducks. I loved them, but instead killed them. What can I do with my feelings?" Therefore, I asked Yu to express my condolences to them, saying, "The eight petals of the lotus platform have been exiled. The double scales of the pearl sea have come out. Their tails are like hibiscus. Their patterns are like tortoiseshell. Their eyes are like amber. Their bodies are like coral. They just crossed the waves and were beautiful. They washed the clear ripples to make them clear. They were already happy and were about to pass away. Suddenly, they were entangled by silkworms and greeted each other. They were killed by peacocks peeping into the mirror. They were confused by the lights of the red finch. Du Fu stood by the bridge and looked into the distance. Su Shi stroked the railing and moved his feelings. I was happy to get two pearls at the same time. Why did the Udumbara flower appear in a flash? Stroking the remains to hurt my soul, I regretted that I could not see this Zhi. Could it be that the oriole crossed the Ji and the Mac crossed the Wen? European Tour Newsletter (57) 191

Matisse's Sixtieth Birthday (D)

Matisse broke away from the examples of Moreau and Rembrandt. He gradually abandoned habitual laws such as "compositional balance" and "tonal reduction." He did not transform the faces of the characters in the book because of the "plastic" concavity and convexity caused by light and darkness. He used thick brushstrokes, skillful lines, and the carvings of a palette knife to show people the deep taste of decoration on the drawing board.

He focuses on pure, unmixed tones, arranging them at equal densities on their irreplaceable light qualities. Comparing him to the art of Édouard Manet is an extreme of perception. Paul Signac (a representative of Neo-Impressionism, still alive and the leader of the Independent Salon) reasonably explained the direct line between the two periods of the French school in his book "From Delacroix to Neo-Impressionism." But he neglected the last leg. In fact, the road to victory is from Delacroix to Matisse. Matisse's colors are not based on scientific theory, but entirely on self-observation, emotional connections, and experiential experience. Like Signac's painters, stimulated by Delacroix's works, he paid attention to the principle of complementary colors. His scientific knowledge directly gave him a certain color. Matisse worked hard to use the color tones that could generate his own emotions to modulate. But his color tones also have a necessary proportion. Sometimes, for this reason, he has to change the shape of the characters, and the structure is also modified. Because of these, everyone called him the leader of the Fauvist school twenty years ago. In fact, the superb coloring of the Fauvist school is their characteristic.

Matisse is a colorist in the sense of glass painting, but not in the sense of Rubens (the Dutch master is good at using gorgeous colors). The lines are gone. Beyond the scope of color, he broke through the color tones. Just like bullet marks that broke the glass, it makes the reader feel the primitive painting. The flat structure of his outline is all Arabian style. The tendency of line drawing and the norm of rhythm all have a kind of dynamic vitality in Matisse's works, just like an electric wire with current passing through it. This primitive rhythm gives the form a system of simplification. It is because the exaggeration of depicting deformed characters often makes the characters in his paintings synthesize and deform. Matisse himself has said, ["If you draw a woman's body, first, you must make her beautiful and meaningful. The rest of the things will come out of this. Relying on the main line, try to extract the meaning of that body as much as possible. At first glance, the surface is not very attractive, but it is full of greater and more human charm in this image that will gradually stimulate the viewer's heart..."]

Matisse purely considers the decorative effects of linear, color, and composition to create. In order to pursue pure artistic inspiration, he used extremely strong contrasting colors. After his sixtieth birthday, he followed Gauguin to Tahiti in South Africa on March 1. I think that in the future, he will definitely have many works praising the exotic customs and expressing the scenery of the South. Perhaps the brush of this genius will make the French style of painting turn to the primitive style of Egyptian stone carvings.
